Current Commentary

The Issue of Our Country Obtaining a Semi-Permanent Seat on the League of Nations Council 11

— Lang

On the 27th of last month, the Committee on the Allocation of Council Seats of the League of Nations Administrative Council met in Geneva. After two days, it passed the recommendation of Lord Cecil, the British representative, and submitted a report to the Administrative Council proposing to increase the number of non-permanent seats on the Administrative Council from nine to eleven, with one of the newly added seats being granted to China, a country in the Asian continent, for a term of three years. This recommendation should be accepted by the upcoming Administrative Council meeting on the 11th of this month. By the time of the League of Nations General Assembly in September, China will likely re-enter the Administrative Council and occupy a council seat.

Why did the Committee on the Allocation of Council Seats of the Administrative Council recommend increasing the number of council seats and granting a seat to China? To explain this issue, we must mention the history of our country's bid for a seat on the League of Nations Council. Since joining the League of Nations, our country has been elected to the Administrative Council a total of three times, and has also failed to be re-elected or re-elected three times. The last time our request for re-election failed was in 1934. According to the method passed by the League of Nations, a non-permanent council member state that requests re-election within three years after the expiration of its term must first obtain the consent of two-thirds of the member states for the right to re-election before it can participate in the election. In fact, it is quite difficult to obtain a two-thirds majority of the votes. The year before last, our country's request for the right to re-election failed by a shortage of 21 votes. Since the right to re-election was not obtained, we were fundamentally unqualified to participate in the election. The Chinese government, in light of the lessons learned from the failure of the election the year before last, immediately changed its approach and submitted a request for a semi-permanent council seat at last year's League of Nations General Assembly. This request was not accepted by the League of Nations, but the Administrative Council only passed the organization of a 14-nation committee to discuss China's request and the allocation of council seats. This committee met last year to solicit opinions from the governments of various member states. Recently, it convened another meeting and passed a report recommending to the Administrative Council to increase the number of non-permanent council seats by two and grant one seat to our country. This is the origin of the resolution of the 14-nation committee. Whether the Administrative Council and the League of Nations General Assembly can accept the report of this subcommittee cannot be predicted at this time. However, judging from the recent situation, there is an 80% to 90% chance that our country will regain a seat on the non-permanent council after September.

Will China's upcoming election as a council member have any impact on ourselves and world peace? This depends on our own efforts in the future. We all know that the League of Nations was originally a group of powerful imperialists when it was first established. However, in recent years, due to the successive withdrawals of aggressors from the League of Nations and the accession of the Soviet Union and Turkey, the League of Nations has become a mechanism for mitigating the outbreak of war and an important factor in the collective security system. Therefore, China's upcoming election as a council member is naturally a manifestation of the increase in peaceful forces, because China is an extremely peace-loving country. However, the prestige and power of the League of Nations have been greatly diminished in recent years due to repeated destruction by aggressors, and China itself is a victim of aggressors. Not only can it not make much contribution to the League of Nations, but it also needs the League of Nations to help it. If we want the League of Nations to become a powerful mechanism for maintaining peace and an important pillar of the collective security system, and to be worthy of being a council member, we must first strengthen our own strength and be able to resist aggression and sacrifice for the future of peace. This will not only save ourselves from the depths of misery, but also indirectly increase the strength of the League of Nations and consolidate the power of the collective security system. If not, China's election as a council member will not have much practical significance.

Sino-American Economic Talks Conclude: Only Silver Agreement Reached, Others Pending 12

(Washington) Reliable sources here claim that the talks between Finance Minister H.H. Kung and the Chinese banking delegation led by Chen Guangfu will result in a silver agreement on currency issues between the two countries. Commercial loans and Sino-American trade issues will be discussed later or pursued through diplomatic channels. It is also uncertain. The talks are now in the final stages, and all technical work by financial experts has been completed. Only a final meeting between the representatives is awaited before the agreement can be reached. If the Finance Minister has time, it should be completed within this week. (1st, Kuo Min Telegraph)

Kwantung Army Chief of Staff Itagaki Arrives in Tokyo, Says He Carries Important Mission 13

(Tokyo) Kwantung Army Chief of Staff Lieutenant General Itagaki arrived in Tokyo on the 30th to attend the Chief of Staff Conference and meet with central figures such as Minister of the Army Terauchi, Chief of General Staff Nishio, and Director Umezu, reporting on the current situation on the border, the state of Soviet Russian Far East military preparedness, and proposing opinions on strengthening the Kwantung Army, and examining specific matters. Itagaki's visit to Tokyo today, accompanied by three staff officers, Takeshita, Hanaya, and Chida, reveals the importance of his mission. Regarding the current state of Japan-Manchukuo relations, Itagaki said: "The Soviet-Manchukuo border issue will be resolved by starting with the eastern border region, establishing a dispute settlement committee and a border demarcation committee to conduct diplomatic negotiations. The Soviet Union illegally extended the border line during the Fengtian warlord era and when Manchukuo's power had not yet reached the border. The Manchukuo government must clarify the truth about this." Negotiations on the Mongolia-Manchukuo border incident are currently being conducted using wireless telegraphy as a preliminary step. In connection with the reorganization of the South Manchuria Railway (SMR), there are plans to unify the operation of all railways owned by the SMR, Manchukuo's railways, and Korean railways. Related authorities are considering the policy. (1st, Domei News Agency)

Italian Troops Pressing Towards Capital - Emperor and Empress Flee - Plan to Escape to Palestine on British Warship - League of Nations Officials Find Themselves in a Dilemma 14

(London) The British Minister to Abyssinia, Mr. Barton, reported to the Foreign Office via wireless today that the Emperor had left the capital. The city is now filled with cries and rampant looting, plunging it into a state of anarchy. Most foreigners have now fled into the embassy area. At the same time, the powerless radio station in the Abyssinian capital has also temporarily ceased communication this morning. Barton also stated that the embassy area in the Abyssinian capital is now in a dangerous state. Therefore, Barton hopes that Italian troops can enter the city tomorrow to maintain order. Currently, only 250 Indian infantrymen and five machine guns are responsible for maintaining the embassy area. Although there are obstacles such as barbed wire and enough food for three months, the defensive strength is far from sufficient. It is said that the ministers of various countries here will return to their countries once the Italian troops arrive. According to today's news, the Italian troops have now advanced to Aijesa, 35 miles from the Abyssinian capital. (2nd National Telegram)

(London) Minister Bardun stationed in Abyssinia telegraphed that the Emperor, Empress, and Crown Prince have now left the Abyssinian capital for Djibouti. Before fleeing, they met at the British Legation, saying that organized resistance in Abyssinia was almost over. Gunfire and looting have now occurred in the Abyssinian capital. It is reported that the British Minister did not advise the Emperor to leave the capital, and the Emperor did not specify where he was going when he left. There are a thousand British people in the city, mostly Indians and Somalis, who have taken precautionary measures to protect themselves. As for the Caucasian British people still staying in the Abyssinian capital, there are only about thirty of them, who are said to have taken refuge inside the British Legation. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

(London) The government received a telegram from Sir Baden, the Minister to Abyssinia, at 1:00 PM today, stating that the Emperor of Abyssinia now intends to lead the royal family and entourage through French-controlled Djibouti, taking a British warship to the British Mandate of Palestine, and specifically requested assistance. The government immediately consulted the French government on whether they had any objections to the Abyssinian Emperor's passage. The French government also replied that they had no objections, but stated that the Djibouti authorities were unable to prepare in time to provide effective protection for the Abyssinian Emperor's safety and hoped that the Emperor would not stay there. The British government has now dispatched a warship, ordering it to set sail immediately to Djibouti, in order to escort the Abyssinian Emperor to Palestine. (2nd Havas Telegram)

Abyssinian Capital: The Abyssinian government will move west. The Emperor met with the diplomatic corps this afternoon to discuss preventative measures to protect foreigners when Italian troops enter the city. (1st Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) According to reliable news from the front, the Italian troops currently advancing northeast of the Abyssinian capital on the Humeidi Plain have encountered torrential rain and muddy roads, forcing them to temporarily halt their advance. (2nd National Telegram)

(Geneva) The Emperor's flight from the Abyssinian capital has placed the League of Nations in an unprecedented predicament. League of Nations members are now very embarrassed. If the League of Nations Covenant is to be maintained, the League of Nations should continue to impose sanctions on Italy. However, Italy will now be able to forcefully argue that the Emperor is a usurper. It is expected that London and Paris will hold diplomatic consultations before the League of Nations Council meeting on May 11 to seek a kind of understanding, and will probably also consult with Italy. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

Abyssinian Capital Has Not Yet Fallen - The Emperor Returned to the Capital from the Front Lines 15

(Paris) According to a telegram from the Abyssinian capital this afternoon, Abyssinian soldiers shot down an Italian plane 20 miles from the capital. The plane caught fire upon landing, indicating that the Abyssinian capital has not yet fallen. (1st Reuters Telegram)

Abyssinian Capital: Our correspondent, Aochainat, reports that although Italian troops are currently advancing victoriously, approaching the Abyssinian capital, the Emperor suddenly returned to the capital today. His spirit of struggle remains as strong as ever. Recently, there have been many rumors and speculations about the Emperor's whereabouts. Some in Europe have even said that the Emperor had been killed at the front lines, which proves to be unfounded. Before entering the capital, the Emperor climbed a high hill outside the city, overlooking the entire city, and talked with various ministers and generals. He descended the mountain and entered the city at 4:00 PM, saying to our correspondent, "The Italian troops are still far from complete victory. Although the Italian troops on both the north and south routes have achieved victories in terms of depth, the breadth of our country is very wide from east to west. In terms of breadth, the Italian troops' progress is insignificant. You must know that there is more than one main road running across a country. If the enemy only advances along one of these roads, how can it be said that this country has been conquered?" However, although the Emperor has returned, those in charge do not conceal the seriousness of the current situation. It is generally believed that the Italian troops are currently heading straight for the Abyssinian capital, encountering no resistance along the way. Upon hearing the news of the Italian troops approaching the capital, foreigners in the capital were all greatly alarmed. European residents do not dare to stray far from their respective embassies, so that they can take refuge in the embassies when the Italian troops enter the city. The mayor and the police department have also prepared everything to maintain order. The embassies of various countries have also agreed to come forward to assist and provide protection when the time comes. (30th Havas Telegram)

Abyssinian Capital: Before leading 5,000 members of the Imperial Guard to the mountains today, the Emperor met with reporters and stated that if necessary, "we will abandon the capital. This matter is not of great importance, because we will build a new capital in the south." He also said, "I am determined not to negotiate directly with the Italians. Our country will use the League of Nations as the only avenue for peace talks. I am determined not to abandon the country, but will all the countries of the world abandon my country and allow it to be controlled by evil fate?" He also said, "Abyssinia will never beg for peace. I am determined to reorganize my forces to fight the Italians. The war between us and the Italians is not only not over, but will continue from now on." According to reporters who witnessed the Emperor, the Emperor's appearance is now quite aged, his beard and hair are already gray, and both hands are bandaged with white cloth. It is said that this is the result of burns caused by Italian poison gas. (1st National Telegram)

Italy Prepares to Celebrate - Final Victory in the War Achieved in Seven Months 16

(Rome) Many places in Italy are celebrating today upon hearing the news of the fall of the Abyssinian capital. The celebrations are especially lively in the north, with crowds gathering in the streets. All shops are closed and all houses are flying flags. Today's newspapers all printed in large letters the news that Italian troops are 60 miles from the Abyssinian capital, saying that the war, which began on October 3 last year, has lasted for seven months, and now Italian troops have reached the gates of the Abyssinian capital. Heavy rain and landslides on the front lines have blocked the Italian troops' advance. Engineers are now busy clearing the streets. Well-informed sources predict that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will announce new peace terms within days. (1st Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) All the people of Italy expect to take the Abyssinian capital in a very short time. It is reported that two routes of Italian troops are now very close to the Abyssinian capital. Previously, heavy thunderstorms and landslides had blocked the road through the Tuma Bai mountain pass, which is 5,000 to 9,000 feet high, preventing the main force from advancing. Now, engineering teams have opened a road with shovels and explosives to allow heavy vehicles to pass. Italian East African Commander-in-Chief Badoglio has traveled south from Tai Xi to participate in the grand ceremony of the Italian troops entering the Abyssinian capital. It is reported that the railway between the Abyssinian capital and Djibouti has now been stopped. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) Frontline news reports that a column of Italian troops on the southern route, led by General Nasi, has occupied the town of Daga Pu. This town is the last defensive line on the road to Harar. Now that it has fallen, the city of Harar has no defenses. As for the northern route, the Abyssinian capital can be taken in a very short time. Various Fascist groups here are now preparing to celebrate. However, the news that Italian troops have already entered the Abyssinian capital has been denied by those in charge. (1st Havas Telegram)

(London) With the rapid advance of Italian troops in Abyssinia and the Abyssinian capital about to fall, political figures here believe that the Abyssinian resistance is extremely weak, and the time for Italy's decisive victory is not far away. It is likely that the Abyssinian government will move south to Gore, which is located in the mountains on the border between British Egypt and Sudan. The terrain is difficult and dangerous, allowing for a long-term defense. Even in the event of ultimate failure, due to its proximity to British territory, there is no need to worry about finding a place to seek refuge. At this time, official figures have not expressed their opinions on the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, but it is generally believed that the government definitely intends to end the dispute in the shortest possible time, because rumors of the merger of Germany and Austria are rampant. Although it is believed by most that German Fuhrer Hitler does not intend to take violent action, but intends to make a request to decide the future of Austria through a plebiscite by the Austrian people, the increasingly tense Manchurian diplomatic situation is difficult to deny. Britain's eagerness to end the Italo-Abyssinian dispute is a plan to devote all its attention to European issues. However, Lord Davis, a member of the House of Lords, will visit Foreign Secretary Eden next Monday on behalf of the joint League of Nations groups to propose a blockade of the Suez Canal, in the hope of cutting off Italy's transportation with East Africa. On the religious side, there is also increased pressure to intensify sanctions against Italy. Both of these will stimulate Italian emotions and make it difficult to resolve the dispute. Political figures believe that if France can come forward to mediate and seek a peaceful solution to the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, then its task, although not easy to accomplish, is also in line with the times and welcomed by Britain. (1st Havas Telegram)

Heavy Casualties on Both Sides - Italian Troops Advance According to Plan 17

(Rome) Lieutenant General Badoglio, Senior Commissioner and Commander-in-Chief of the Expeditionary Force of Italian East Africa, recently issued Public Bulletin No. 200, stating that the troops under the command of General Nasir Pu, Commander-in-Chief of the Abyssinian Southern Route Army, were defeated by our country at the town of Sasabana and are now fleeing towards the city of Qiqihaga. In this battle, the Abyssinian army suffered a total of 5,000 casualties. Since launching the offensive on the 14th of last month, the Italian army has suffered only 50 officer casualties and 1,800 soldier casualties. As for the northern route, a column of Italian troops, after occupying the city of Makefote, recently crossed the Gabala Rapids and is now no more than 100 kilometers away from the Abyssinian capital. Other troops have also advanced from Teburada Po, the capital of the Begmedet Province, and have occupied the cities of Teburashina and Terma Ba Mountain Pass. (1st Havas Telegram)

(Rome) According to today's public announcement from the Italian Commander-in-Chief, Italian troops are continuing to advance according to the planned strategy. The Abyssinian army on the southern front is currently in collapse. Italian troops are temporarily concentrated in the already occupied positions in order to continue the advance. Many chiefs of Upper Wokaden have now surrendered to the Italian army and are willing to cooperate with the Italian army to eliminate the Abyssinian army. After receiving the report of the Emperor's flight, British Foreign Secretary Eden immediately went to the Foreign Office to consider the overall situation. Since the League of Nations has not invited the Emperor to attend the League of Nations meeting to be held in Geneva on May 11, and the rumor that the Emperor will come to England has not been confirmed, it is not yet known whether the Abyssinian cabinet members have also left the capital with the Emperor. It is also impossible to determine what impact the Emperor's flight will have on the situation in the Abyssinian capital. It is not known whether the Italian troops will ask foreign residents, including the British Minister, to leave the country when they arrive in the Abyssinian capital. It is reported that the British Minister, Barton, has not yet made a decision to leave the city. The Abyssinian Embassy in England stated that it has not received news of the Emperor's departure from the capital. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

The Emperor Was Almost Killed by Rebel Soldiers 18

Abyssinian Capital: The Emperor today called on all men in the country who can fight to go to the front lines on the northern route, preparing five days' worth of military supplies, in order to prevent Italian troops from attacking the capital. General Gai Taichu will be the commander. The Emperor was recently almost killed by rebels. According to General Koni Falov, an advisor to General Gasa, rebels in Malaga fired at the Emperor and his entourage, killing a servant standing next to the Emperor and a guard officer. The Emperor was not injured, which is truly remarkable. The Abyssinian capital is now almost completely empty, except for the police who maintain order. At the same time, Abyssinian men residing in French Djibouti have been ordered to report for military service in the Abyssinian capital. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

Various Countries Peacefully Celebrate Labor Day - Soviet Russia Holds Grand Military Parade - Hitler Still Says He Desires Peace - Tokyo Imposes Martial Law, Prohibiting Workers' Parades 20

(London) The celebration of May Day around the world saw few disturbances. The largest demonstration was held in Moscow, where 30,000 soldiers and 1.5 million citizens marched past Stalin. 300 tanks followed in the procession, and 700 aircraft soared through the sky. All commerce and entertainment were suspended throughout Spain. Public affairs and cafes were closed all day. Laborers in Sofia held a mass rally under government guidance. There were clashes between demonstrators and police in the Durboji area, resulting in three deaths. Paris and London passed quietly. (1st Reuters Telegram)

(Berlin) This afternoon, Hitler drove through the city to the former imperial palace to speak to the people. Germany's goal is peace. His speech was broadcast nationwide by radio. The celebration of May Day this afternoon was exceptionally lively. Regulations restricting taverns were relaxed for three days. They were all full, and many did not close their doors all night. This afternoon, 2 million people cheered Hitler along the route he passed. When Hitler appeared on the balcony of the Prime Minister's residence in the evening, thousands of more people cheered him. Today's celebration culminated in a splendid torchlight military parade. (1st Reuters Telegram)

(Berlin) Today is German Labor Day. Cabinet ministers and Economic Minister and President of the German Reichsbank, Schacht, participated in the celebrations in Lustgarten. A large number of employers and workers from various industries attended, all lined up in a grand display. Fuhrer Hitler then delivered a speech, reiterating Germany's desire for peace. He said, "We all know that peace is necessary for Germany and other countries. If a war were to break out in Europe, it would not benefit us in the slightest. We desire peace and want to achieve that goal, but we hope that other countries will not hinder it. For three years, we have reached out to other countries whenever we have had the opportunity, no less than a dozen times. The world is saying that Germany intends to attack the Czech Republic and Austria." At this point, Fuhrer Hitler asked, "Who does not want peace?" The audience responded loudly, "The Jews, the Jews!" Fuhrer Hitler continued, "Let the enlightened people of all countries listen to this. We know from experience that peace is a perfect and beautiful thing, but the unity of our country must be maintained, because the unity of Germany is a guarantee of human order, peace, and culture, and is also a guarantee of European civilization." (1st Havas Telegram)

Only 50,000 members of the Socialist Party and Communist Party, who recently organized a united front to oppose war and fascism, held an orderly parade here. (1st National Telegram)

(Paris) This month's Labor Day passed peacefully without any incidents. All public utilities in the city, except for hired automobiles, operated as usual. Another 6,000 people held a rally in the Chrisi stadium. Various places in the provinces, such as Bordeaux, Brest, Nantes, Strasbourg, Lyon, and Lille, were also orderly and peaceful. Although workers held parades and sang the Internationale, and many public transportation services were shut down, no accidents resulted. (1st Havas Telegram)

U.S. House of Representatives - Passes Massive Naval Budget - Over 531 Million Gold Dollars - To Build 102 Warships 21

(Washington) The House of Representatives has passed the naval budget bill, with a total amount of 531,068,707 dollars, which is the largest naval budget in peacetime. The House of Representatives also authorized the government to immediately begin construction of two battleships to match the other signatory countries of the Anglo-French-American naval treaty when they build battleships to replace old ships. The intended uses for the funds stipulated in this budget bill are as follows: To complete the 84 warships currently under construction; To add 12 destroyers and 6 submarines; To strengthen naval aviation capabilities; Raw materials needed by the navy in wartime should be stockpiled in a timely manner. (1st Havas Telegram)

(Washington) After the House of Representatives Appropriations Committee reported the naval budget bill today, it suddenly and unexpectedly considered the bill and will try to pass it by the end of this week. House Majority Leader Bankhead declared that new developments had occurred, so it was necessary to consider the bill immediately. The House will convene a special meeting on Saturday of this week to discuss the bill. The Appropriations Committee's report approved a peacetime naval budget of 531,068,707 dollars to build 12 destroyers, 6 submarines, 2 battleships, and 330 aircraft, and stipulated that the naval personnel be increased from 88,000 to 96,500, and the Marine Corps be increased from 16,000 to 17,000. The provision to build two battleships will only take effect when the signatory countries of the 1930 or 1936 London Agreement engage in the construction of battleships. The Committee stated in its report that the United States should be one of the last countries to participate in the arms race, but if other countries initiate a naval construction competition, the United States will definitely not be left behind. (30th National Telegram)

(Washington) The House Appropriations Subcommittee previously held a closed-door meeting to discuss the unprecedented naval appropriations bill. Rear Admiral Taussig of the Navy made an important statement, outlining the reasons why the bill must be passed. The statement was not released until today. According to reports, Taussig participated in the Boxer Rebellion in China in 1900. He stated that Japan is currently implementing a program of large-scale naval and air force expansion and is modernizing its existing battleships and light cruisers. Japan's naval power in the East is increasing day by day. The United States, due to the independence of the Philippines, has fewer interests in the East than before, and the British naval position overseas is also weaker. In light of this situation, the Dutch government is greatly concerned about the security of the Dutch East Indies. Taussig also said that the U.S. fleet will mostly be stationed in the Pacific in the next 12 months and will conduct large-scale exercises there every year. (30th Reuters Telegram)

Germany Actually Concludes a Commercial Agreement with Puppet Manchukuo, Valid for One Year 23

(Tokyo) It is learned today that Germany and "Manchukuo" have concluded a new commercial agreement stipulating that "Manchukuo" may, within twelve months from June 1st of this year, transport products worth 100 million Japanese yen into Germany. Germany will pay three-quarters of the value of these goods in foreign currency (Japanese yen), and the remaining quarter in Marks. "Manchukuo" agrees to use these Marks to pay for German products imported into "Manchukuo." If Germany's exchange position cannot enable the Foreign Exchange Office to raise 75 million Japanese yen in foreign currency, the products "Manchukuo" exports to Germany may be reduced, but limited to 65 million Japanese yen, and no lower. Payment will still be made according to the aforementioned method. According to some provisions, Japan's trade surplus with Germany can be offset in part by the increased exports from "Manchukuo" to Germany. If this commercial agreement needs to be continued, negotiations should begin before April 1, 1937. (2nd Reuters Dispatch)

(Berlin) Representatives of the German Foreign Exchange Administration and corresponding agencies on the "Manchukuo" side today signed a German-"Manchukuo" commercial agreement to facilitate the expansion of trade between the two parties. This is the result of the German economic delegation's visit to the Far East under the leadership of Dr. Kipp. At the same time, German Economics Minister Dr. Schacht and the head of the Soviet Russian commercial delegation also concluded an agreement to adjust Russian-German trade and handle payment solutions for this year. (30th Reuters Dispatch)

(Berlin) Regarding the German-Manchukuo commercial contract signed by the German economic survey mission, Berlin government officials declared that anyone who claims this purely commercial agreement has any political implications is trying to create ill will towards Germany. Germany is the largest customer for Manchurian soybeans and naturally wants to import more German goods into Manchuria in exchange for the lowest possible price for soybeans, hoping to meet the needs of the entire country. Germany lacked fat and butter last winter, mainly due to the shortage of soybeans, and the purpose of this agreement is nothing more than to improve this situation. (2nd National Telegram)

Zhejiang-Jiangxi Specialty Exhibition, Pre-Exhibition Opens in Hangzhou 27

(Hangzhou) The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Specialty Joint Exhibition Pre-Exhibition held its opening ceremony at the Hangzhou Commodity Exhibition Hall at 2:00 PM on the 1st. The pre-exhibition will last for two weeks and close on the 14th, after which all exhibits will be transported to Jiangxi, and Jiangxi specialties will be transported to Zhejiang. Internal Ministry Implements Trial Staff Greeting Rituals 28

(Nanjing) The Ministry of the Interior, in view of the declining social customs in recent years and the lack of etiquette, which has been ridiculed by foreigners, believes that not only the general public, but also staff in various agencies pay little attention to etiquette. Often, staff members in the same department are indifferent to each other when they meet. In order to correct this bad habit, the Ministry has formulated staff greeting rituals and will first implement them internally on the 1st to see the effectiveness before promoting them to other agencies and the whole country. The draft of the greeting rituals stipulates that lower-level staff must bow to the Minister and senior staff when they meet and take their leave. The Minister and senior staff must also return the greeting. After the greeting, they must also greet each other, with phrases such as "How are you (or How do you do)?", and responses such as "Fine," "Very well." When male and female staff meet, if they shake hands, the female staff should extend her hand first. The etiquette during memorial weeks and other gatherings stipulates that all staff should stand up and salute when the Minister enters the room. When someone is troubled, they must express "Thank you," "Many thanks," etc. to the other party. If there is any abruptness, they must express "Sorry," "Excuse me," etc. to the other party. (2nd Central News Agency Telegram)

Constitution Draft Approved, Legislative Yuan Discussion Situation 30

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 59th meeting on the 1st, morning and afternoon, and passed the third reading of the draft constitution amendment, with a total of eight chapters and 148 articles, which will be submitted to the Central National Government tonight for announcement as scheduled on May 5th. 68 legislators attended the meeting on the 1st. President Sun Ke and Ye Chucang arrived at the Yuan at around 7:00, but did not attend. At the start of the meeting, Fu Bingchang first reported on the review process, which lasted one and a half hours. Then the second reading began. Chapters 1, 2, and 3 were all passed without objection. Article 44 of Chapter 4, originally "When the state encounters an emergency or a major economic change, and rapid action is required, the President may, after deliberation by the Executive Yuan, issue an emergency order to take necessary measures. The preceding item that must be decided by the Legislative Yuan shall be submitted to the Legislative Yuan for ratification within two months after the order is issued." Lü Zhiyi believed that the term "situation" was too abstract and easily misleading. After the members expressed their opinions successively, the amendment was passed. Regarding the period for submitting to the Legislative Yuan, some advocated changing three months to one month, but it was ultimately believed that the essence of this provision was to comply with the procedures for requesting ratification, and not the length of time, so it was not changed. The original Article 45 of the Five-Yuan Presidents' Conference stipulated that "The President may convene a conference of the presidents of the five yuan to decide on the following matters: 1. Matters that cannot be resolved between yuan. 2. Matters submitted by the President that relate to two or more yuan." Shi Shangkuan, Fu Bingchang, Wu Jingxiong, Xu Yuangao, Zhong Tianxin, Chen Changheng, and others all expressed their opinions. The chairman declared a 15-minute recess due to the complexity of the issue, and an eight-member committee reported on the sorted issues. After continued discussion, there was still debate, with some saying that the Five-Yuan Conference violated the legacy of the five-power independence. However, after Fu Bingchang explained that this was not a permanent institution and was only to resolve disputes between two or more yuan, it was deemed not to violate the legacy. Then the chairman explained in detail and advocated not using a conference to resolve disputes, but adopting the method of the British Prime Minister inviting cabinet members to a meeting. The amendment was passed. There were objections to Article 58 regarding the concurrent positions of the President and Vice President of the Executive Yuan, but it was not passed. In Article 67, Chen Changheng and Guan Suran proposed increasing the number of members from Mongolia, Tibet, and Overseas Chinese from six to eight, and in Article 87, Liang Hancao advocated that the power to discipline civil servants be transferred to the jurisdiction of the Control Yuan for further study, but because there were few supporters, it was not passed. After the discussion of Chapter 4 was completed, the meeting was extended to 2:30 PM to continue the discussion. Articles 109 and 128 were each amended by only one word. Article 130 originally had "However, usage fees collected for the passage of boats and vehicles due to the improvement of land and water roads are not subject to this restriction." Zheng Hongnian was afraid of abuses and advocated deleting it. The chairman agreed with the common opinion, so it was agreed to delete it. Article 131, "Education funds that are independent according to law shall be protected by a team." Chen Changheng and Liu Zhendong advocated deleting it because education funds should be planned as a whole, but there were few supporters, so it was not modified. Article 140, "Laws that conflict with the constitution are invalid. In the preceding situation, the Control Yuan shall, within six months after the law is implemented, submit a clear explanation to the Judicial Yuan, which shall be detailed in the law." Some advocated deleting the second item, and some advocated deleting it completely. After the chairman explained, they agreed to retain it, but the four words "in the preceding situation" were modified. Article 143, regarding the creation of legislators and supervisors during the transition period, half of them are appointed by the President upon the recommendation of the President of the Yuan, but legislators have the restriction of "selecting those with specialized knowledge and experience," while supervisors do not. After debate, the restriction on legislators was deleted. After that, there were no objections to each article. After the second reading was completed, Zhong Tianxin raised awareness of how to remedy the situation when the President is vacant, because there are no such provisions in Articles 51 and 53. It was then passed to add the first item "When the President is vacant, the Vice President shall succeed to his office" in Article 51. The amended articles were then given a third reading, and the remaining third reading procedures were omitted, and it was unanimously passed at 4:45 PM. Then, the National Assembly Representative Election Law was discussed, but it was not fully reviewed. It was decided to continue the discussion on the morning of the 2nd. (1st Central News Agency Telegram)

Tashiro Succeeds as Commander of the Japanese Garrison in North China, Tada Transferred to the 11th Division Commander 31

Fan suffered three serious injuries, Yang suffered a serious injury to his right elbow, rendering it immobile, and Ma also suffered several injuries. When Harding was committing the assault, Fan, Yang, and Ma were greatly surprised by the sudden attack and did not fight back, fearing that the hunting dogs would run out and bite the children. Prince De Telegraphed Beiping to Deny Inner Mongolia Independence; However, a Certain Country's Plot for Mongolia Is Very Urgent; Mongols Resent Jun Sheng's Murder 42

Beiping Dispatch The rumors of Inner Mongolia's independence have been repeatedly proven false. However, on the 28th of last month, it was rumored again in Beiping that Prince De would organize an Inner Mongolia Autonomous Government, appointing himself as chairman, with six ministries established, and the ministers were also decided. Currently, all the ministers are in Prince De's Mansion, (Pangling) discussing everything, and they can be announced at an appropriate time. Each ministry will have two or three departments, and each department will have three sections. The selected ministers for the six ministries are: Yu Shan Jue Lang, Minister of General Affairs; Hori Ming, Minister of Military Affairs; Murata Matsu, Minister of Finance; Hiroshima Shiro, Minister of Education; Ari Saburo, Minister of Transportation (all Japanese); and Baolada Dalifu (Mongol), Minister of Justice.

After the above news was released, it attracted great attention from all parties. Bao Yueqing, director of the Mongolian Political Council's office in Beiping, and Ao Yunzhang, acting secretary-general of the council in Beiping, telegraphed Prince De's Mansion in Bailingmiao on the 29th to inquire about the truth. At 8:30 a.m. on the 30th, they received Prince De's telegram reply, stating that the rumors were absolutely untrue. Thus, the cloud of uncertainty disappeared. However, a certain party's plot for Mongolia is not a recent development. They have indeed sent more than 20 advisors, sitting in Prince De's Mansion in Pangling, urging Prince De. Prince De is currently in his mansion, feeling deeply trapped due to the adverse environment. Although his will is firm, the environment is very difficult. Since Eastern Mongolia was occupied, the people of Inner Mongolia have disapproved of the Japanese actions. Even the recently murdered Mongolian Jun Sheng, former governor of the puppet Beixingan Province, was from a prominent Mongolian family with great wealth. He had been in the Northeast for many years. The charge for his murder was collusion with the enemy (Soviet Russia). In reality, Jun Sheng had always disapproved of the Japanese atrocities and did not collude with Russia. His murder aroused resentment among other Mongolians. At the same time, the Xilinguole League in Western Mongolia (headed by Prince De) borders Outer Mongolia. A certain party fears that Prince De will therefore become closer to Russia, so they are pressing him even harder. Judging from this, the future of Western Mongolia is not optimistic. (1st Day)

Tianjin Smuggled Goods Piling Up; Sales Obstructed, Prices Plunge; Ross Visits Tianjin to Meet Kawagoe 44

Tianjin Dispatch The authorities have not yet formally promulgated new measures to prevent smuggling in North China due to various concerns. However, since the return of Customs Superintendent Lin Shize from Nanjing to Tianjin, he has consulted with Tianjin Customs Commissioner Xu Liya and the authorities of the Beining and Jinpu Railways, and has begun to implement effective first-step measures based on the instructions of the Ministry of Finance. These measures began on April 27th, with the establishment of tax checkpoints in Cang County (Jinpu Railway) and Changxindian (Pinghan Railway), and inspection stations at the Xiaozhakou confluence of the North and South Grand Canal and Ziya River in the suburbs of Tianjin. Both land and water routes are strictly controlled to prevent smuggled goods from being transshipped from Tianjin to the south. In addition, more than 100 informants have been hired at high salaries to spread throughout the city and outside, and they immediately secretly notify the customs of any smuggling, and the customs quickly intercept the goods. The 29th Army, the Hebei Provincial Fifth River Water Police Bureau, and the police are all assisting in this effort. If the ronin resist, they are forcibly executed. Therefore, although the number of smuggled goods coming from East Hebei in recent days has not decreased compared to the past, it is true that the smuggling of these goods from Tianjin to the inland is no longer as rampant as before. Furthermore, according to investigations, the inventory of smuggled rayon currently stored in Tianjin is as high as 800,000 bundles or more. Due to the obstruction of sales, the original prices have fallen steadily. Tianqiao brand is only selling for 87 yuan, Tantan brand is only selling for 92 yuan, and miscellaneous brands are only selling for 80 yuan, which is a drop of 60 to 70 yuan per piece compared to a month ago. A bag of sugar is now selling for only 16.5 yuan, which is a drop of 5 to 6 yuan compared to before. These are the local prices after smuggling into Tianjin. As for those transported to Zhoucun in Shandong, Gaoyang in Hebei, and along the Pinghan and Jinpu Railways, rayon sells for 180 yuan per bundle and a bag of sugar sells for 19.5 yuan. After deducting transportation costs, the profit is very little. If smuggling is carried out secretly, there is still some profit to be made. However, customs enforcement is now strict, and it is not easy to transship goods secretly. If regular taxes are paid and goods are transported, more goods will be transported due to the lower tariffs. As a result, each sales location will inevitably be overloaded, and those in the business will have to lower prices to sell off, and will eventually engage in mutual squeezing and end up with no profit. Therefore, they are deeply concerned that lower tariffs will affect the future of smuggling. The smuggling ronin have recently been unable to profit from smuggling. The stockpiled goods have also caused losses of capital and interest. In the past week, the total losses are estimated to be more than 100,000 yuan. In order to quickly clear out their smuggled goods, the ronin have sent people to southern Hebei, western Shandong, Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai to solicit business from shops in those areas. Therefore, since last week, some smuggled goods have been transported from Tangshan through land to Chahar and then sold to the Northwest. It is expected that in the near future, the Northwest provinces will also become the end market for smuggled goods.

The situation of smuggling in North China is as described above. It has been learned that the British economic expert Sir Frederick Leith-Ross has come to Tianjin again to interview various parties about this matter. Sir Frederick arrived in Tianjin on the 26th. After arriving in Tianjin, he refused to meet guests. According to the British consulate, his visit was a private action and he would not visit any parties. He left for Beijing on the 28th. However, according to investigations, the meaning of Sir Frederick's trip to the north is entirely to investigate the quiet situation of smuggling in North China and the current situation of British commercial economy. On the 27th, he convened British merchants and tycoons to inquire about everything. In the afternoon, he visited the Customs Commissioner of the Tianjin Customs, Xu Liya, for a long talk. Before leaving Tianjin on the 28th, he visited the Japanese Consul General's residence in the British Concession at 9:00 a.m. and asked Japanese Consul General Kawagoe about smuggling in North China. Sir Frederick said that too many smuggled goods were being transported, the North China economic market was chaotic, and Japanese goods were monopolizing the market. The British merchants were losing their market. Japan had the intention of directly threatening British economic power in China. Kawagoe said that the rampant smuggling was due to the inevitably high Chinese tariffs. If, as in South China, Japanese goods were given preferential treatment, this would not happen. Sir Frederick said that China's tariff rates were recently planning to reduce. He had made some suggestions, which would be adopted by the Chinese government. Kawagoe said that this was a matter for the Chinese government and he had no right to interfere. Sir Frederick finally hoped that Kawagoe would pay attention to anti-smuggling and prevent changes in British commerce. Kawagoe pointed out that this matter was within the purview of the Tianjin Customs, and the Japanese side could not interfere. Sir Frederick further pointed out that Japan was obstructing the execution of the central government's policies by the Hebei-Chahar political authorities and had unified the currency system in China. He asked if there was any intention of doing this. Kawagoe replied that so far, he had not heard of any such facts. After the meeting, Sir Frederick visited the Japanese Commander Tada, and also exchanged opinions on the previous matter, but still did not obtain any key information, so he hurriedly went to Beiping. Recently, because the wind of smuggling has not been suppressed, British and American businesses have suffered greatly. If this continues, it is impossible to do anything. Sir Frederick Leith-Ross will soon return to Shanghai, or make suggestions to our government.

Last year, the total customs revenue in North China was 40 million yuan. The 24th year is about to end, and although there are no detailed statistics on tax revenue, it is predicted that it will be less than last year. The reasons for this include rural bankruptcy, a sharp decline in imported goods, and the low gold price in the first half of the year, which affected the customs gold unit. The most important reason is the excessive number of smuggled goods. Because of the reduced customs revenue, the guarantee for foreign debt will undergo drastic changes. Tianjin Customs Commissioner Xu Liya will probably go to Shanghai recently to contact Customs Director-General Frederick Maze. (30th Day)

Smuggled Goods Invade Shandong; Rayon Floods Zhoucun; Weavers Greatly Affected 45

Jinan Dispatch Smuggled goods from North China have gradually invaded southern Shandong Province. Zhoucun, east of Jinan, used to be the center of the silk weaving industry, with numerous weaving houses, and was known as Little Hangzhou. After the decline of the silk industry, many rayon goods were woven, and sold far and wide. In recent days, it has been greatly oppressed by smuggled rayon. It is said that these smuggled rayon goods all originate from Yatsushiro and are transshipped through Jinan to Zhoucun, unloading 400 to 500 boxes per day, with each box worth more than 120 yuan. Because they are smuggled goods, they are cheap, and people flock to them. Each day, tens of thousands of yuan flow out. This rayon is worth 4 or 5 yuan per piece in Japan. When transported to Zhoucun, each piece can be sold for 11 or 12 yuan. Because the profit is so great, the smugglers are like madmen. In previous years, the silk weaving business in Zhoucun was relatively stable. Because most of the rayon came from official goods, the cost was slightly higher, so there was no great frenzy in the market. Recently, it is completely smuggled goods, resulting in unstable market prices and daily drops. Each piece has fallen from 17 yuan to 13 yuan. Merchants in this city, because the price of rayon has fallen by more than 80 yuan per box compared to before, believe that it will rise again in the future. Whether they are in the industry or not, they have purchased and stockpiled them. However, smuggled goods are coming in an endless stream. As of April 29th, each piece has fallen to 10 yuan, causing those who stockpiled at 12 or 13 yuan before to lose 50 or 60 yuan per box, and they are constantly complaining. Judging by the trend, it is likely to break through the 10 yuan mark. Because of the falling price of raw materials, the goods woven by each weaving house are piled up like mountains and no one asks about them. The city's finances are gradually drying up and stagnating due to more outflow than inflow. If this continues, the market will be in an unspeakable state. (1st Day)

Shanxi Provincial Bandit Suppression Army Implements Blockade of Remaining Bandits; Bandits Gather Dispersed Troops to Occupy Western Shanxi; National Army Builds Forts for Strict Defense and Decisive Encirclement 46

Taiyuan Dispatch The bandit suppression military affairs in Shanxi Province have entered a state of ceasefire in various sectors in recent days. Regarding the bandit suppression strategy, the authorities have recently reached an agreement with the first and second Route Commanders Chen Cheng and Yang Aiyuan after several deliberations, and it seems that some changes have been made. Since the recovery of various counties along the Datong-Puzhou Railway in southern Shanxi, as well as Xingxian and Linxian counties in northern Shanxi, the bandits have suffered heavy losses after repeatedly crossing the river to disrupt Shanxi. With no way out, they have gathered scattered troops and prepared to withdraw their troops and return to their base. Therefore, bandits from various routes have gathered in Yonghe, Daning, Puxian, Fenxi, Xixian, Xiaoyi, and Shuangchi Town in Lingshi along the river in western Shanxi, under the personal command of bandit leaders Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, and Lin Biao. They are also deploying military forces. On the other hand, puppet political workers are going out to win over people and promote communism, with the intention of occupying the above-mentioned counties as temporary bases and making another attempt to make a comeback. The bandits believe that since entering Shanxi, they have suffered successive defeats, their strength has been weakened, and replenishment is difficult. The initial attempt has not been successful as hoped. Recently, the Shanxi-Suiyuan armies and the Central troops have been advancing steadily, deploying carefully, and the strength is far from what the bandits can match. With no hope of advancing and no way to retreat, the only way for the bandits to return is to their old nest in northern Shaanxi. However, all the river crossings have been blocked by the Shanxi army in advance, and on the west bank of the river, the Shaanxi side has also mobilized a large army to deploy defenses along the river. Zhang Xueliang, Deputy Commander of the Northwest Bandit Suppression, and Yang Hucheng, Director of the Xi'an Pacification, and other senior generals have all personally deployed and supervised the suppression. Therefore, it seems not easy for the bandits to return even if they want to. The bandits are in a dilemma, and therefore have the cunning plan of temporarily occupying western Shanxi to observe the situation. The National Army, in view of this, deeply believes that it is unfortunate that the bandits are disrupting Shanxi, but it is absolutely undesirable to let them return to northern Shaanxi to harm the people of Shaanxi. The fundamental solution is to cut off the fuel under the cauldron and eliminate them all. However, although the bandits are a rabble, they are not enough to accomplish anything, but there are many party members, and if they want to eliminate them all in one fell swoop, they must adopt other effective methods. Therefore, the current changed strategy is to use the situation of the bandits occupying western Shanxi to redeploy the National Army in the vicinity, assigning heavy troops to guard the areas near the bandit areas and along the Datong-Puzhou Railway, to be responsible for local guards and searching for scattered bandits. The remaining large armies are all moving to the bandit areas in western Shanxi, taking a heavily surrounded position. At the same time, strongholds are being secretly built in various key passes in the bandit areas to strengthen defenses. Most of the construction and deployment have been completed. Commander Chen Cheng of the Road recently went to Lingshi and summoned senior military officers of the Central Army to meet, which was to personally give instructions on this strategy. After this formation is completed, even if it is not possible to completely eliminate all the bandits immediately, if the bandits want to wander around, commit rape and plunder, it is feared that it will be an impossible delusion. Moreover, the counties in western Shanxi have obstructed transportation, the land is barren, and the people are poor. Even in times of good harvest, the residents work hard all year round, and 90% of them cannot get enough to eat and wear. The state of their impoverished livelihood often makes people gasp when they talk about it with people in those areas. The state of peace is still like this. In recent years, the rural areas of Shanxi Province have generally been in economic panic, and of course the counties in western Shanxi are the worst. Furthermore, this time the communist bandits are disrupting Shanxi, and the above-mentioned counties have once again borne the brunt. After several battles, they have been ravaged by the bandits, and it has become barren and miserable. Most of those with some assets or abilities have long since fled. In this kind of scene that is no longer human, the bandits still want to occupy it as a base, and it can be said that they will not be able to rely on it for long.

The bandits are extremely panicked because the National Army's encirclement has been completed. The 2,000 to 3,000 bandits led by Xu Donghai, who occupied Daimaijiao in Xixian and Shuangchi Town in Lingshi, have fled south under the leadership of Xu. It is estimated that they are eager to jump out of the cage and open up a new path. However, the strength of the bandits has been damaged and their morale has been low. It is feared that their next move will inevitably be a fierce battle with the Shaanxi army on the opposite bank, in an attempt to return to northern Shaanxi. (30th Day)

Songjiang; Jinshan Public Group Retains Captain 47

Hong Pinlan, captain of the First Company of the Thirteenth Battalion of the Jinshan Security Corps, had previously been granted a one-month extension of training due to illness, and had been instructed to comply with an order from the district commander on April 4. However, yesterday, it was suddenly reported that Captain Hong had not recovered from his long illness and should be dismissed. Subsequently, Wang Qiyuan, a standing committee member of the Jinshan County Anti-Smoking Committee, Lu Xiao, district chief of the first district, Zhu Xalu, chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, and Tang Zhengdong, chairman of the Rescue Grand Alliance, telegraphed the Security Office from Songjiang yesterday to request the retention of Hong.

However, County Magistrate Wu ignored this and left without saying anything. Transfer of Jurisdiction in the Zhu Xiongwu Case 50

Zhu Xiongwu, a former clerical official in the Jiangsu High Court, was reported for falsely claiming to represent the Jiangsu Judicial Reform Association and for making arrogant pronouncements and slanderous remarks against the President of the High Court, Zhu Shusheng. He was arrested and detained by the Wuxi District Court upon order. Later, it was discovered that Zhu was involved in a fraudulent household registration case, implicating former High Court clerk Chen Chaozuan, lawyer's clerk Lu Wenguang, and several legal and lawyer figures in Shanghai and Wuxi. The Wuxi District Procuratorate summoned and questioned them separately. As a result of the investigation, Zhu, Chen, Lu, Wuxi District Court bailiff Xu Dunben, and Chen Chaozuan's wife, Li, were indicted in the same court's criminal division, with the trial scheduled to begin on the 14th of this month. However, Zhu argued that since the accusations against him were made by President Zhu of the High Court, there might be unfairness in the trial. He petitioned the Supreme Court for a ruling to transfer jurisdiction. The Supreme Court's Third Criminal Division has now ruled in favor of the transfer to the Shanghai Special District Local Court for trial. Therefore, all witnesses and involved parties in the case will soon be escorted to Shanghai for adjudication.

Estimated Spring Silkworm Cocoon Production in Wuxi 51

The Wuxi Silkworm and Silk Testing Center, in conjunction with various guidance stations, has been actively promoting silkworm rearing for this spring season. All silkworm eggs have been collected and distributed to silkworm farmers for rearing. The number of silkworm egg sheets distributed from the silkworm farming demonstration area is 174,209, more than double the amount from last spring and approximately 70% more than the 106,135 sheets distributed in the autumn season. It is expected that farmers' interest in silkworm rearing has increased this year, and the sale of silkworm eggs by merchants has decreased. The total number of silkworm eggs reared this spring, including those sold by merchants, is estimated to be over 300,000 sheets. If the weather is favorable and there are no drastic changes, the yield of fresh cocoons could exceed 100,000 piculs (担), equivalent to 30,000 piculs of dried cocoons. In addition, Zhou Jixian, a technician dispatched by the Silkworm Industry Improvement Association, has completed his inspection in Wuxi and returned to the provincial capital to report. Furthermore, since 1934, the Provincial Silkworm Industry Improvement Association has been implementing a unified control system for silkworm eggs and cocoon trading, which has been effective in reducing consumption and improving quality. Therefore, the association will continue to actively implement this system in 1936. To increase silk production, the promotion of mulberry seedlings is considered urgent. A large number of mulberry seedlings were purchased from Zhejiang Province last year and distributed to farmers for planting at no cost, totaling more than 2 million plants. This year, mulberry seedlings will also be cultivated on barren land within the province to achieve self-sufficiency.

Changzhou: Adulterous Woman Murders Husband 52

In Xiejiabiao Village, near Xueyanqiao Town, in the eighth district of Wujin County, a farmer named Qin Cannian married a woman named Qin, who was naturally promiscuous. The couple's relationship was poor, and they often argued. On the morning of the 30th, neighbors suddenly heard of Cannian's sudden death, causing great suspicion. However, they were all afraid of Qin's fierce and overbearing nature and did not dare to investigate. Lu Jingzu, the head of the Xin'nan Township, upon hearing the news, went to investigate with the Baojia chief. Qin initially refused them entry, but Township Head Lu and others ignored her and examined the body, discovering a knife wound in the throat, clearly indicating that the promiscuous woman had murdered him before his death. It is unknown whether others were involved in the murder. Township Head Lu immediately ordered Qin to be placed under surveillance. Qin submitted without objection and was escorted to the Eighth District Office in Caoqiao Town. District Chief Xie Yingzheng reported the case to the local court that evening. Today (the 1st), Prosecutor Guan Junjie went to the village to examine the body and investigate the case.

Zhangjiagang, bordering the northern part of Jiaxing and belonging to Jiangsu Province, has many winding harbors where bandits frequently appear. Local News

Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries Invited Financial Circles Yesterday to Discuss the Establishment of the Agricultural Capital Bureau; Outline of Measures Passed; to Be Established on July 1st; Soliciting Opinions from the Banking Sector, to Be Compiled and Submitted to the Ministry by a Deadline 54

Minister Wu Dingchang of the Ministry of Industries invited leaders of the Shanghai financial community to discuss the establishment of the Agricultural Capital Bureau at the Bankers' Association Club at 59 Hong Kong Road yesterday afternoon. An outline of measures was passed, and it was resolved to establish the bureau on July 1st. Details are as follows:

Representatives Present

The following representatives attended yesterday: Minister Wu Dingchang of the Ministry of Industries, Chen Xing of the Central Bank, Xi Demao, Ye Zhuotang of the Central Trust Bureau, Li Shuming of the Central Savings Society, Song Hanzhang of the Bank of China, Bei Songsun, Zhang Xinyi, Zhu Lengbo, Tang Shoumin of the Bank of Communications, Zhang Peishen, Li Zhongchu, Hu Mengjia of the China Industrial Bank, Lu Zidong of the Jiangsu Bank, Du Yuesheng of the Chung Hwa Bank, Xu Xinliu of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Qian Xinzhi of the Four Banks Savings Association, Shi Bozhao, Zhu Runsheng of the China Farmers Bank, Wu Muhan of the Donglai Bank, Fan Jimei of the Enterprise Bank, Wang Boyuan of the Ken Yeh Bank, Qi Yunqing of the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Xu Hanqing of the Continental Bank, Hu Bijang of the Zhongnan Bank, Mei Zhezhi of the Agricultural and Commercial Bank, Chen Yingsheng, Zhou Zuomin of the Jincheng Bank, Wu Yunzhai, Yu Zuoting of the Ningpo Commercial & Savings Bank, Wang Yansong of the Silk Industry Bank, Qu Jigang of the Guohua Bank, Wu Xizhi of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, Zou Bingwen of the Shanghai Bank, Yang Jiemei, Li Fusun of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Wang Zhixin of the New China Bank, Ge Yanhe of the Yien Yieh Commercial Bank, and 27 other banks, as well as Lin Kanghou of the Shanghai Banking Association and 39 other people.

Meeting Proceedings

First, Minister Wu Dingchang of the Ministry of Industries, as chairman, reported: "Regarding the Ministry's joint establishment of the Agricultural Capital Bureau with various banks, I invited everyone to a discussion meeting on the 13th of last month to report on the outline of measures for the Agricultural Capital Bureau and solicit opinions from the banking community. At the same time, on the 28th of last month, I had a detailed discussion with experts familiar with the actual situation of agricultural economics, including Zou Bingwen, Wang Zhixin, Zhang Xinyi, and Li Zhongchu, and revised the outline. Regarding the capital portion, in addition to the fixed capital of 30 million yuan to be allocated by the government, a joint investment of 30 million yuan will be borne by the participating banks, with 6 million yuan to be paid annually over five years. The circulating capital has no fixed amount and will be determined by negotiation between the participating banks. The Agricultural Capital Bureau plans to be established in Nanjing, with a board of directors to manage it. Branches will be established in important locations, and commissioners will be stationed in each county." He then read out the revised outline, which was unanimously approved. As for any opinions from the banking community on the Agricultural Capital Bureau, please submit them to the Shanghai Banking Association for compilation and submission to the Ministry before May 15th. It was also resolved to establish the bureau on July 1st. The meeting adjourned at approximately 6 PM.

Outline Passed

Outline of measures for the Agricultural Capital Bureau: In order to circulate agricultural funds, adjust agricultural products, and thereby develop rural areas, the government, in conjunction with various banks, is specially establishing the Agricultural Capital Bureau. The Agricultural Capital Bureau will operate with the following types of funds: (A) Fixed capital: 30 million yuan, to be allocated by the government at the beginning of each fiscal year, starting from 1936, with 6 million yuan to be allocated each year for a total of 30 million yuan over five years. (B) Joint investment capital: 30 million yuan, to be paid by the participating banks at the beginning of each fiscal year, starting from 1936, with 6 million yuan to be paid each year for a total of 30 million yuan over five years. (C) Circulating capital: No fixed amount, to be determined by the Agricultural Capital Bureau in consultation with the participating banks at the beginning of each year and as needed. In addition to the above funds, when necessary, the government may order the Agricultural Capital Bureau to issue agricultural bonds, with the government responsible for guaranteeing the principal and interest. The Agricultural Capital Bureau's affairs are divided into two parts: agricultural materials and agricultural products. (A) Agricultural materials: (1) Establish agricultural banks, cooperatives, or peasant pawnshops in various counties and rural areas. Those that are approved by the Agricultural Capital Bureau and deemed to require assistance may be invested in and promoted with 1,000 to 10,000 yuan from the fixed capital, and the bureau will be responsible for supervision and inspection. (2) Mortgage loans for general agricultural products may be made by utilizing fixed, joint investment, and circulating funds separately. (3) Local agricultural banks, cooperatives, or peasant pawnshops may re-mortgage the mortgaged items obtained from loans to the Agricultural Capital Bureau to borrow fixed capital or joint investment capital, and to participating banks to borrow circulating capital. (4) The Agricultural Capital Bureau may, upon decision by the board of directors,酌借 (zhuó jiè, carefully borrow) funds to improve agricultural products. The interest rate on the above loans shall be determined by the board of directors according to local customs and may be adjusted to a certain extent as a reserve fund. In case of losses on loans, the reserve fund may be used to cover the losses first. The above business shall be determined by the board of directors separately, in terms of operating regulations and the order of their implementation. (B) Agricultural products: (1) Disposal of agricultural products in mortgaged items. (2) General purchase and sale of agricultural products. (3) Acting as an agent for the general purchase and sale of agricultural products. (4) Entrusted by the government to act as an agent for the purchase and sale of agricultural products. (5) Operating warehouses and negotiating with various railway bureaus to build warehouses for low-cost rental. The above business shall be operated with fixed capital, in addition to borrowing joint investment capital and circulating capital through mortgage or acceptance methods. The above business shall be determined by the board of directors separately, in terms of operating regulations and the order of their implementation. The Agricultural Capital Bureau is to be established in Nanjing, with ten directors selected by the government and ten directors elected by the participating banks to form a board of directors. The government will appoint one president and two vice presidents from among the directors to manage the bureau's affairs under the direction of the Ministry of Industries. Branches may be established in important locations, and commissioners will be stationed in each county. The organizational regulations for the Agricultural Capital Bureau shall be separately determined by the Ministry of Industries. The regulations regarding the freight rates for agricultural products on state-owned railways and ships and the tax rates for agricultural products at the central and local levels must solicit the opinion of the president of the Agricultural Capital Bureau. In case of disagreement, the president may submit a request to the government to send personnel to adjudicate. The Agricultural Capital Bureau may, according to the output and traffic conditions of agricultural areas in various provinces, be divided into five zones, to be handled in separate years and completed within five years. The profits and losses of the Agricultural Capital Bureau shall be borne by the government. (A) For fixed capital, any surplus at the time of the annual final accounting shall be used to increase its amount, and any losses shall be made up for. (B) The joint investment capital shall bear interest at a rate of 8% per annum, with the Agricultural Capital Bureau guaranteeing the principal and interest. Participating banks, etc., may include it under the statutory agricultural loan item. The Agricultural Capital Bureau shall issue joint investment capital certificates, which may be used as collateral and may be transferred to other financial institutions with the permission of the Agricultural Capital Bureau. If there is a surplus in the Agricultural Capital Bureau's annual final accounting, participating banks that have contributed joint investment capital will be rewarded. (C) Circulating capital shall be recovered at any time according to its terms, duration, and interest rate.

Record of the Drawing of the Fuguoquan Lottery the Day Before Yesterday: All 1,717 Winning Numbers Drawn in Fifteen Hours; First Prize 06402, Fundraised by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for the Lumber Industry Association; Lay Buddhist Yao Attended to Supervise, and Lin Jinyu Personally Came to Supervise the Drawing 61

The Shanghai Goods Aid and Revitalization Association held the drawing of the Fuguoquan Lottery the day before yesterday (the 1st) at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Auditorium. More than 500 people attended, making it a grand occasion. Lay Buddhist Yao from Suzhou also attended to supervise. Lin Jinyu, President of the Shanghai Auditing Bureau of the Control Yuan, personally came to supervise the drawing. A total of 1,717 winning numbers were drawn, with the entire drawing completed at 2 AM, lasting fifteen hours. The first prize, number 06402, was fundraised by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for the lumber industry association. Details are as follows:

Drawing Order

The drawing was originally scheduled to begin at 10 AM, but was delayed until 11 AM while waiting for Lay Buddhist Yao to arrive. The order was as follows: 1. All attendees stood at attention. 2. Music was played. 3. The attendees paid their highest respects to the Party, National Flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen. 4. Sun Yat-sen's last will and testament was respectfully read. 5. The attendees observed a moment of silence. 6. The Chairman of the Committee gave a report. 7. The Committee members gave a report. 8. The Standing Committee member and Director of the Office gave a report. 9. The supervisor gave a speech. 10. Guests gave speeches. 11. Photography. 12. The balls were checked and put in to the drawing machines. 13. The drawing began. 14. The winning numbers were announced. 15. The meeting adjourned.

Chairman's Report

At 11 AM, after announcing the start of the drawing and performing the ritualistic bow, Chairman Zhu Qinglan of the Committee reported, roughly stating, "Ladies and gentlemen, the association is very honored by your presence to watch the drawing today. The association, supported by Lay Buddhist Yao from Suzhou, who devoted her family fortune to aid the revitalization, established an office on March 8th. To maintain credibility, we have been busy and meticulous, and in these short fifty-odd days, we have made preparations and are holding the drawing on schedule today. However, it was originally scheduled to begin at 10 AM, but it is now later because Lay Buddhist Yao has devoted her family fortune to aid the revitalization, and she has come to Shanghai to participate in this grand opening ceremony. We had to wait for her arrival, which is why the opening is later. In addition, when Ms. Yao made the donation, she stated that the purpose was to revitalize northern Jiangsu by 80,000 yuan, which has now been done. Of the 120,000 yuan of Fuguoquan Lottery proceeds, 80,000 yuan will go to northern Jiangsu, and the remaining 40,000 yuan will be used elsewhere."

Director's Report

Standing Committee member and Director of the Office Cheng Jingsheng then reported, roughly stating, "Today, due to the pressing time for the drawing, I apologize for not being able to report more fully. Please allow me to briefly explain. 1. All 12,000 Fuguoquan Lottery tickets were fully subscribed. 2. We received generous donations of goods from various benefactors, which are generally sufficient. 3. The exhibition of donated items for the public to view, as well as the invitation of evaluation experts to evaluate the prizes and allocate them, are all past events. Now, after the drawing, we will distribute the items. Please claim your prizes according to the winning numbers. Today, we are borrowing the drawing balls from the Central Savings Society to show our prudence. As for the allocation of calligraphy and paintings as prizes, I dare not say that it is appropriate, because some donors were too modest and marked the prices too low, and the association could not increase them on their behalf. Items from those who were generous and those who were modest were placed together, so the allocation of prizes will inevitably be uneven. Also, within the same rank, the order of priority was based on the order in which the items were received, not on whether the top items were fine pieces and the bottom items were inferior pieces. This needs to be stated. Also, the prize list is difficult to compile, and the prize distribution date was originally set for May 4th, but it may not be possible in time and will have to be postponed for a few days, which will be announced in the newspaper at that time."

Supervisor's Speech

The supervisor, Lin Jinyu, Director of the Shanghai Auditing Office of the Control Yuan, stated, "All lottery drawings should pay attention to being solemn, fair, and impartial. For the sake of prudence, the Auditing Office has sent me here personally." Zhang Yipeng from Suzhou then gave a speech. After the speeches, Director Lin inspected the number balls and poured them into three bronze balls, A, B, and C, to start the drawing.

Drawing Proceedings

The Fuguoquan Lottery drawing balls were borrowed from the Central Savings Society, with three bronze balls, A, B, and C. Ball A contained numbers from 100 to 1300, totaling 1200 number balls. Ball B contained numbers from 0 to 90. Ball C contained 12 balls representing the prize ranks. Because the Fuguoquan Lottery had a total of 12,000 tickets, divided into special prizes and regular prizes, with the special prizes divided into 12 ranks and the regular prizes divided into 5 ranks, the prize ranks were drawn first, and then the corresponding numbers were drawn. The first number drawn was for the 12th prize, totaling 802 numbers. The first prize was drawn at 1:30 AM, with the winning number 06402, fundraised by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for the lumber industry association. The remaining winning numbers are listed in today's advertisement, so I will not repeat them here.

Supervisory Personnel

The supervisory personnel present that day, in addition to representatives from various agencies and the association's Chairman Zhu Ziqiao and Standing Committee members Cheng Jingsheng and Wang Yiting, included Wang Xiaolai, Lin Jinyu, Lin Kanghou, Yu Zuoting, and others. Lay Buddhist Yao also arrived at the venue at 11:00 AM, accompanied by Mrs. Nie Yuntai and others.

Eight Types of Old Government Bonds to Be Exchanged, Starting the Day Before Yesterday 62

The Zhejiang Provincial Government is issuing 60 million yuan in consolidated government bonds to exchange for eight types of old government bonds. The bond regulations have been submitted to the Executive and Legislative Yuans for approval and will be issued starting on May 1st. The old bonds to be exchanged include the 1928 Repayment of Old Debts Government Bond, the 1928 Highway Government Bond, the 1929 Construction Government Bond, the 1930 Disaster Relief Government Bond, the 1931 Clearance of Old Debts Government Bond, the 1932 Treasury Bills, the 1934 Local Government Bond, and the 1930 Hangzhou Waterworks Government Bond. The bonds are being printed by the China Bookstore and other printers in the city. Once the printing is complete, the Zhejiang Provincial Government will entrust various banks to exchange them. The method is the same as the Ministry of Finance's exchange of consolidated government bonds. Interest due on the 9th installment of the treasury bills and the 13th installment of the construction government bonds that matured on April 30th will be paid as usual. However, the principal of the treasury bills will not be paid temporarily and will be reissued when the new bonds are exchanged.
